			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SWE_improve_the_stridsvagn_122"
			if = {
				#Get a new tank tech and some new tanks.
				limit = { NOT = { has_tech = MBT_4 } }
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = MBT_4
					amount = 20
					producer = SWE
				}
				set_technology = { MBT_4 = 1 }

				#If you already have the tech, you get some more tanks to still have a viable focus.
				else = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = MBT_4
						amount = 40
						producer = SWE
					}
				}

				GER = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {

					}

					OR = {
						original_tag = EUU
					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = eurosceptic
						value = -0.1
					}
					if = {

							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }

						value = 0.20
					}
					if = {

							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }

					}

							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}

							check_variable = { eurosceptic < 0 }

						original_tag = EUU
					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = eurosceptic
						value = 0.3
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {

							check_variable = { eurosceptic < 0 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }
					}
			}
					set_country_flag = focus_EU102_maj
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				date > 2001.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.4
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -40
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
		}
	}

									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }

							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				date > 2010.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}

				add = -10

					has_country_flag = focus_EU301_QMV_yes
					has_country_flag = focus_EU301_maj_yes

		continue_if_invalid = yes
		available_if_capitulated = no
		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_focus_EU301
			hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = EUU
					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = eurosceptic
						value = -0.1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic < 0 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }

					}

					}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = EUU
					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = eurosceptic
						value = 0.3
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {

							check_variable = { eurosceptic < 0 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }
					}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = european_federation
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU301_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU301
			}
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				date > 2004.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.4
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -40
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
		}
	}

						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic < 0 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }
					}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = EUU
						original_tag = ENG
					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = eurosceptic
						value = 0.3
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic < 0 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }
					}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = european_federation
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU306
			}
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
						modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}

							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }

									value = v

										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }

										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }

				set_country_flag = focus_EU403

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				date > 2003.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than

					}

						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than

					}

		}

				add = 40

			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {

							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals

					}

				limit = {
					has_global_flag = european_federation
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU601_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU601
			}
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				date > 2004.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.4
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}

					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}

					}

					OR = {
						original_tag = EUU
					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = eurosceptic
						value = 0.3
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }

						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }
					}
			}
					set_country_flag = focus_EU110_maj
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
						modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.4
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -40
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
		}
	}

									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {

							var = eurosceptic

						}
					}
